######################################################################
# Valid arguments:
#
# area = [nation/culture/nation_culture/nation_religion/religion/all]
# government = [monarchy/republic/theocracy/anti/any]
# defection = [culture/culture_group/religion/any/none]
# independence = [culture/culture_group/religion/colonial/any/none]
# gfx_type = [culture_province/culture_owner]
#
######################################################################

# All rebels in province scope

# For siege_won_trigger, siege_won_effect
# FROM = owner
# ROOT = province

# For Other
# FROM = owner
# ROOT = Homecountry
######################################################################
# Pagan rebels. Disgruntled fanatics.
######################################################################
pagan_religion_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = pagan_religion
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = pagan_religion }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = pagan_religion
			owner = { religion = pagan_religion }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = pagan_religion }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = pagan_religion
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pagan_religion
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pagan_religion }
			}
			change_religion = pagan_religion
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pagan_religion
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = pagan_religion }
			}
			change_religion = pagan_religion
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

baltic_pagan_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = baltic_pagan
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = baltic_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = baltic_pagan
			owner = { religion = baltic_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = baltic_pagan }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = baltic_pagan
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = baltic_pagan
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = baltic_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = baltic_pagan
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = baltic_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = baltic_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = baltic_pagan
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence

	reinforcing = yes

	artillery = 0.0

	cavalry = 0.3

			factor = 1.5

			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = tengri_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = tengri_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = tengri_pagan
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}
zun_pagan_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = zun_pagan
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = zun_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = zun_pagan
			owner = { religion = zun_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = zun_pagan }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = zun_pagan
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = zun_pagan
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = zun_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = zun_pagan
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = zun_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = zun_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = zun_pagan
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bon
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = bon }
			}
			change_religion = bon
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}
bon_reformed_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = bon_reformed
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = bon_reformed }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = bon_reformed
			owner = { religion = bon_reformed }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = bon_reformed }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = bon_reformed
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bon_reformed
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = bon_reformed }
			}
			change_religion = bon_reformed
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bon_reformed
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = bon_reformed }
			}
			change_religion = bon_reformed
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

		}

			factor = 0.0

		}

			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}

			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }

			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {

			controlled_by = REB
		}

	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}

		}

	}

		always = yes

	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = kushitism_pagan_reformed
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = kushitism_pagan_reformed }
			}
			change_religion = kushitism_pagan_reformed
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}
magyar_pagan_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = magyar_pagan
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = magyar_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = magyar_pagan
			owner = { religion = magyar_pagan }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = magyar_pagan }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = magyar_pagan
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = magyar_pagan
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = magyar_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = magyar_pagan
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = magyar_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = magyar_pagan }
			}
			change_religion = magyar_pagan
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pagan_religion_reformed }
			}
			change_religion = pagan_religion_reformed
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pagan_religion_reformed
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = pagan_religion_reformed }
			}
			change_religion = pagan_religion_reformed
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

######################################################################
# Christian rebels. Disgruntled fanatics.
######################################################################
cathar_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = cathar
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = cathar }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = cathar
			owner = { religion = cathar }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = cathar }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = cathar
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cathar
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cathar }
			}
			change_religion = cathar
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cathar
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { religion = cathar }
			}
			change_religion = cathar
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bogomilist
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { religion = bogomilist }
			}
			change_religion = bogomilist
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

monothelite_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = monothelite
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = monothelite }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = monothelite
			owner = { religion = monothelite }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = monothelite }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = monothelite
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = monothelite
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = monothelite }
			}
			change_religion = monothelite
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = monothelite
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { religion = monothelite }
			}
			change_religion = monothelite
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = messalian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { religion = messalian }
			}
			change_religion = messalian
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

adamites_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = adamites
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = adamites }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = adamites
			owner = { religion = adamites }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = adamites }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = adamites
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = adamites
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = adamites }
			}
			change_religion = adamites
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = adamites
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { religion = adamites }
			}
			change_religion = adamites
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = kharijite
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
				NOT = { religion = kharijite }
			}
			change_religion = kharijite
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

druze_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = druze
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = druze }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = druze
			owner = { religion = druze }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = druze }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = druze
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = druze
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = druze }
			}
			change_religion = druze
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = muslim
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = druze
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
				NOT = { religion = druze }
			}
			change_religion = druze
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {

			units_in_province = 1
		}

		}

		religion_group = muslim

		}
	}
}
alawite_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = alawite
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = alawite }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = alawite
			owner = { religion = alawite }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = alawite }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = alawite
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = alawite
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = alawite }
			}
			change_religion = alawite
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = muslim
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = alawite
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
				NOT = { religion = alawite }
			}
			change_religion = alawite
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

######################################################################
# Mazdan rebels. Disgruntled fanatics.
######################################################################
mazdaki_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = mazdaki
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = mazdaki }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = mazdaki
			owner = { religion = mazdaki }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = mazdaki }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = mazdaki
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mazdaki
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mazdaki }
			}
			change_religion = mazdaki
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = zoroastrian_group
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mazdaki
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				NOT = { religion = mazdaki }
			}
			change_religion = mazdaki
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

khurmazta_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = khurmazta
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = khurmazta }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = khurmazta
			owner = { religion = khurmazta }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = khurmazta }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = khurmazta
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = khurmazta
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = khurmazta }
			}
			change_religion = khurmazta
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = zoroastrian_group
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = khurmazta
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				NOT = { religion = khurmazta }
			}
			change_religion = khurmazta
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0

	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

		}

			factor = 2

		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1

			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1

			controlled_by = REB

	 		}
	 	}

			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4

			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {

				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = gayomarthianism
			}

				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730

		if = {

				NOT = { religion = gayomarthianism }
			}
			change_religion = gayomarthianism

			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

######################################################################
# Gnostic rebels. Disgruntled fanatics.
######################################################################
manichean_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = manichean
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = manichean }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = manichean
			owner = { religion = manichean }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = manichean }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = manichean
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = manichean
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = manichean }
			}
			change_religion = manichean
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = gnostic
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = gnostic }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = manichean
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = gnostic
				NOT = { religion = manichean }
			}
			change_religion = manichean
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = cainitism
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = cainitism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = cainitism
			owner = { religion = cainitism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = cainitism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = cainitism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cainitism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cainitism }
			}
			change_religion = cainitism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = gnostic
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = gnostic }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cainitism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = gnostic
				NOT = { religion = cainitism }
			}
			change_religion = cainitism
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

######################################################################
# Jewish rebels. Disgruntled fanatics.
######################################################################
samaritan_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = samaritan_faith
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = samaritan_faith }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = samaritan_faith
			owner = { religion = samaritan_faith }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = samaritan_faith }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = samaritan_faith
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = samaritan_faith
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = samaritan_faith }
			}
			change_religion = samaritan_faith
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = jewish_group
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = samaritan_faith
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = jewish_group
				NOT = { religion = samaritan_faith }
			}
			change_religion = samaritan_faith
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes

druidism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = druidism
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = druidism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = druidism
			owner = { religion = druidism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = druidism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = druidism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = druidism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = druidism }
			}
			change_religion = druidism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = druidism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = druidism }
			}
			change_religion = druidism
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}
kemetism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = kemetism
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked

		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = kemetism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = kemetism
			owner = { religion = kemetism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = kemetism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = kemetism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = kemetism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = kemetism }
			}
			change_religion = kemetism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {

			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }

			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}

	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = cybelene }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = cybelene
			owner = { religion = cybelene }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = cybelene }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = cybelene
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cybelene
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cybelene }
			}
			change_religion = cybelene
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cybelene
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = pagan
				NOT = { religion = cybelene }
			}
			change_religion = cybelene
			force_converted = yes
		}
	}
}
zamolxism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = zamolxism
	defection = none			# Defects to countries of their religion
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = yes
	gfx_type = culture_province

	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes

	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3

	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes

	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = zamolxism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}

 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = zamolxism
			owner = { religion = zamolxism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = zamolxism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = zamolxism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}

 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = zamolxism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = zamolxism }
			}
			change_religion = zamolxism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		religion_group = pagan
	}

	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	# Localization for their demands
	demands_description = "generic_rebels_demand"

	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = zamolxism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}

	religion = caucasian_pagan
